</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Ragnar_Lodbrok" title="Ragnar Lodbrok">Ragnar Lodbrok</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Ragnar Lodbroks död by Hugo Hamilton.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg/100px-Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="79" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg/150px-Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg/200px-Ragnar_Lodbroks_d%C3%B6d_by_Hugo_Hamilton.jpg 2x" data-file-width="452" data-file-height="356" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr> 865
</td>
<td>Ragnar Lodbrok, a semi-legendary Viking leader whose exploits are narrated in the <i><a href="/wiki/Tale_of_Ragnar_Lodbrok" title="Tale of Ragnar Lodbrok">Ragnars saga loðbrókar</a></i>, a thirteenth-century Icelandic saga, is said to have been captured by <a href="/wiki/%C3%86lla_of_Northumbria" title="Ælla of Northumbria">Ælla of Northumbria</a>, who had him executed by throwing him into a <a href="/wiki/Snakepit" class="mw-redirect" title="Snakepit">pit of snakes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Louis_III_of_France" title="Louis III of France">Louis III of France</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:GrabLudwig_III.jpg" class="image"><img alt="GrabLudwig III.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/GrabLudwig_III.jpg/100px-GrabLudwig_III.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="133" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/GrabLudwig_III.jpg/150px-GrabLudwig_III.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/GrabLudwig_III.jpg/199px-GrabLudwig_III.jpg 2x" data-file-width="576" data-file-height="768" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>5 August 882
</td>
<td>Louis III, king of <a href="/wiki/West_Francia" title="West Francia">West Francia</a>, died aged around 18 at <a href="/wiki/Saint-Denis,_Seine-Saint-Denis" title="Saint-Denis, Seine-Saint-Denis">Saint-Denis</a>. Whilst mounting his horse to pursue a girl who was running to seek refuge in her father's house he hit his head on the lintel of a low door and fell, <a href="/wiki/Skull_fracture" title="Skull fracture">fracturing his skull</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Sigurd_Eysteinsson" title="Sigurd Eysteinsson">Sigurd the Mighty</a> of <a href="/wiki/Orkney" title="Orkney">Orkney</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>892
</td>
<td>Sigurd the Mighty, the second <a href="/wiki/Earl_of_Orkney" title="Earl of Orkney">Earl of Orkney</a>, strapped the head of his defeated foe, <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A1el_Brigte_of_Moray" title="Máel Brigte of Moray">Máel Brigte</a>, to his horse's saddle. Brigte's teeth rubbed against Sigurd's leg as he rode, causing a fatal infection, according to the Old Norse <i><a href="/wiki/Heimskringla" title="Heimskringla">Heimskringla</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Orkneyinga_saga" title="Orkneyinga saga">Orkneyinga</a></i> sagas.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Edmund_Ironside" title="Edmund Ironside">Edmund Ironside</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Edmund Ironside - MS Royal 14 B VI.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg/100px-Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="92" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg/150px-Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg/200px-Edmund_Ironside_-_MS_Royal_14_B_VI.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="601" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>30 November 1016
</td>
<td>Edmund Ironside was allegedly stabbed whilst on a toilet, by an assassin hiding underneath.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/B%C3%A9la_I_of_Hungary" title="Béla I of Hungary">Béla I of Hungary</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:B%C3%A9la_I_(Chronica_Hungarorum).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Béla I (Chronica Hungarorum).jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/B%C3%A9la_I_%28Chronica_Hungarorum%29.jpg/100px-B%C3%A9la_I_%28Chronica_Hungarorum%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="113" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/B%C3%A9la_I_%28Chronica_Hungarorum%29.jpg/150px-B%C3%A9la_I_%28Chronica_Hungarorum%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/B%C3%A9la_I_%28Chronica_Hungarorum%29.jpg/200px-B%C3%A9la_I_%28Chronica_Hungarorum%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="936" data-file-height="1060" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>11 September 1063
</td>
<td>Béla I of Hungary, when the <a href="/wiki/Holy_Roman_Empire" title="Holy Roman Empire">Holy Roman Empire</a> decided to launch a military expedition against Hungary to restore young <a href="/wiki/Solomon,_King_of_Hungary" title="Solomon, King of Hungary">Solomon</a> to the throne, was seriously injured when "his throne broke beneath him" in his manor at <a href="/wiki/D%C3%B6m%C3%B6s" title="Dömös">Dömös</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Turner2011_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Turner2011-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> The King—who was "half-dead", according to the <i><a href="/wiki/Illuminated_Chronicle" class="mw-redirect" title="Illuminated Chronicle">Illuminated Chronicle</a></i>—was taken to the western borders of his kingdom, where he died at the creek Kanizsa on 11 September 1063.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Illuminated_Chronicle_68.96_117_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Illuminated_Chronicle_68.96_117-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Philip_of_France_(1116%E2%80%931131)" title="Philip of France (1116–1131)">Crown Prince Philip of France</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Philip_of_France_(1131).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Philip of France (1131).jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Philip_of_France_%281131%29.jpg/100px-Philip_of_France_%281131%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="106" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Philip_of_France_%281131%29.jpg/150px-Philip_of_France_%281131%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Philip_of_France_%281131%29.jpg/200px-Philip_of_France_%281131%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="301" data-file-height="319" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>13 October 1131
</td>
<td>Crown Prince Philip of France died while riding through Paris, when his horse tripped over a black pig running out of a dung heap.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Henry_I_of_England" title="Henry I of England">Henry I of England</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Henry1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Henry1.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Henry1.jpg/100px-Henry1.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="163" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Henry1.jpg/150px-Henry1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Henry1.jpg/200px-Henry1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="921" data-file-height="1500" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1 December 1135
</td>
<td>While visiting relatives, Henry supposedly ate too many <a href="/wiki/Lamprey" title="Lamprey">lampreys</a> against his physician's advice, causing a pain in his gut and ultimately his death.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Al-Musta%27sim" title="Al-Musta&#39;sim">Al-Musta'sim</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:HulaguInBagdad.JPG" class="image"><img alt="HulaguInBagdad.JPG" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/HulaguInBagdad.JPG/100px-HulaguInBagdad.JPG" decoding="async" width="100" height="59" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/HulaguInBagdad.JPG/150px-HulaguInBagdad.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/HulaguInBagdad.JPG/200px-HulaguInBagdad.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1678" data-file-height="982" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>20 February 1258
</td>
<td>Al-Musta'sim, the last <a href="/wiki/Abbasid" class="mw-redirect" title="Abbasid">Abbasid</a> <a href="/wiki/Caliph" class="mw-redirect" title="Caliph">Caliph</a> of <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>, was executed by his <a href="/wiki/Mongols" title="Mongols">Mongol</a> captors by being rolled up in a rug and then trampled by horses.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Edward_II_of_England" title="Edward II of England">Edward II of England</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_(detail).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Edward II - British Library Royal 20 A ii f10 (detail).jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_%28detail%29.jpg/100px-Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_%28detail%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="99" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_%28detail%29.jpg/150px-Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_%28detail%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_%28detail%29.jpg/200px-Edward_II_-_British_Library_Royal_20_A_ii_f10_%28detail%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="957" data-file-height="944" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>21 September 1327
</td>
<td>Edward II of England was rumoured to have been murdered, after being deposed and imprisoned by his <a href="/wiki/Queen_consort" title="Queen consort">wife</a> <a href="/wiki/Isabella_of_France" title="Isabella of France">Isabella</a> and her lover <a href="/wiki/Roger_Mortimer,_1st_Earl_of_March" title="Roger Mortimer, 1st Earl of March">Roger Mortimer</a>, by having a <a href="/wiki/Horn_(anatomy)" title="Horn (anatomy)">horn</a> pushed into his anus through which a red-hot iron was inserted, burning out his internal organs without marking his body.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> However, there is no real academic consensus on the manner of Edward II's death and it has been plausibly argued that the story is propaganda.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/John_of_Bohemia" title="John of Bohemia">John of Bohemia</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:John_of_Luxemburg.PNG" class="image"><img alt="John of Luxemburg.PNG" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/John_of_Luxemburg.PNG/100px-John_of_Luxemburg.PNG" decoding="async" width="100" height="236" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/John_of_Luxemburg.PNG/150px-John_of_Luxemburg.PNG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/John_of_Luxemburg.PNG/200px-John_of_Luxemburg.PNG 2x" data-file-width="339" data-file-height="800" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>26 August 1346
</td>
<td>John of Bohemia, after being blind for 10 years, died in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Crecy" class="mw-redirect" title="Battle of Crecy">Battle of Crecy</a> when - at his command - his companions tied their horses' reins to his own and charged. He was slaughtered in the ensuing fight.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Charles_II_of_Navarre" title="Charles II of Navarre">Charles II of Navarre</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Charles_II_of_Navarre.png" class="image"><img alt="Charles II of Navarre.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Charles_II_of_Navarre.png/100px-Charles_II_of_Navarre.png" decoding="async" width="100" height="115" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Charles_II_of_Navarre.png/150px-Charles_II_of_Navarre.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Charles_II_of_Navarre.png/200px-Charles_II_of_Navarre.png 2x" data-file-width="356" data-file-height="411" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1 January 1387
</td>
<td>Charles II of Navarre known as "Charles the Bad". The contemporary chronicler <a href="/wiki/Froissart" class="mw-redirect" title="Froissart">Froissart</a> relates that the king, suffering from illness in old age, was ordered by his physician to be tightly sewn into a linen sheet soaked in distilled spirits. The highly flammable sheet accidentally caught fire and Charles later died of his injuries. Froissart considered the horrific death to be God's judgment upon the king.<sup id="cite_ref-Johnston1806b_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Johnston1806b-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Martin_of_Aragon" title="Martin of Aragon">Martin of Aragon</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Martín I de Aragón.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg/100px-Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="137" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg/150px-Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg/200px-Mart%C3%ADn_I_de_Arag%C3%B3n.jpg 2x" data-file-width="835" data-file-height="1140" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>31 May 1410
</td>
<td>Martin of Aragon died from a combination of indigestion and <a href="/wiki/Death_from_laughter" title="Death from laughter">uncontrollable laughing</a>. According to tradition, Martin was suffering from indigestion on account of eating an entire goose when his favorite <a href="/wiki/Jester" title="Jester">jester</a>, Borra, entered the king's bedroom. When Martin asked Borra where he had been, the jester replied with: "Out of the next vineyard, where I saw a young deer hanging by his tail from a tree, as if someone had so punished him for stealing figs." This joke caused the king to die from laughter.<sup id="cite_ref-doran_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doran-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Renaissance">Renaissance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Renaissance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col">Name of person
</th>
<th scope="col">Image
</th>
<th scope="col">Date of death
</th>
<th scope="col">Details
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/George_Plantagenet,_1st_Duke_of_Clarence" title="George Plantagenet, 1st Duke of Clarence">George Plantagenet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Duke_of_Clarence" title="Duke of Clarence">Duke of Clarence</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:George_Plantagenet,_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg" class="image"><img alt="George Plantagenet, Duke of Clarence.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/George_Plantagenet%2C_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg/100px-George_Plantagenet%2C_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="125" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/George_Plantagenet%2C_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg/150px-George_Plantagenet%2C_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/George_Plantagenet%2C_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg/200px-George_Plantagenet%2C_Duke_of_Clarence.jpg 2x" data-file-width="270" data-file-height="337" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>18 February 1478
</td>
<td>George Plantagenet, 1st Duke of Clarence, was allegedly executed by drowning in a barrel of <a href="/wiki/Malvasia" title="Malvasia">Malmsey wine</a>, apparently his own choice once he accepted he was to be killed.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Victims of the <a href="/wiki/Dancing_plague_of_1518" title="Dancing plague of 1518">1518 dancing plague</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Die Wallfahrt der Fallsuechtigen nach Meulebeeck.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg/100px-Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="127" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg/150px-Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg/199px-Die_Wallfahrt_der_Fallsuechtigen_nach_Meulebeeck.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1660" data-file-height="2116" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>July 1518
</td>
<td>In July 1518, several people died of either <a href="/wiki/Myocardial_infarction" title="Myocardial infarction">heart attacks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stroke" title="Stroke">strokes</a> or <a href="/wiki/Fatigue" title="Fatigue">exhaustion</a> during a <a href="/wiki/Dancing_mania" title="Dancing mania">dancing mania</a> that occurred in <a href="/wiki/Strasbourg" title="Strasbourg">Strasbourg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alsace" title="Alsace">Alsace</a> (<a href="/wiki/Holy_Roman_Empire" title="Holy Roman Empire">Holy Roman Empire</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cosimo_Gheri&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cosimo Gheri (page does not exist)">Cosimo Gheri</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;&#91;<a href="https://it.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cosimo_Gheri_(vescovo)" class="extiw" title="it:Cosimo Gheri (vescovo)">it</a>&#93;</span>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>24 September 1537
</td>
<td>According to the <a href="/wiki/Duchy_of_Florence" title="Duchy of Florence">Florentine</a> historian <a href="/wiki/Benedetto_Varchi" title="Benedetto Varchi">Benedetto Varchi</a>, Cosimo Gheri, the 24-year-old <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Fano-Fossombrone-Cagli-Pergola" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Fano-Fossombrone-Cagli-Pergola">Bishop of Fano</a> (<a href="/wiki/Papal_States" title="Papal States">Papal States</a>), died of pain due to the <a href="/wiki/Shock_(circulatory)" title="Shock (circulatory)">shock</a> of having been <a href="/wiki/Rape" title="Rape">raped</a> by <a href="/wiki/Pier_Luigi_Farnese,_Duke_of_Parma" title="Pier Luigi Farnese, Duke of Parma">Pier Luigi Farnese</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Pope_Paul_III" title="Pope Paul III">Pope Paul III</a> (see <a href="/wiki/Rape_of_Fano" title="Rape of Fano">Rape of Fano</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> But the event is far from certain.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Pietro_Aretino" title="Pietro Aretino">Pietro Aretino</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino,_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg" class="image"><img alt="La muerte de Pietro Aretino, por Anselm Feuerbach.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino%2C_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg/100px-La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino%2C_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="153" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino%2C_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg/150px-La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino%2C_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino%2C_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg/200px-La_muerte_de_Pietro_Aretino%2C_por_Anselm_Feuerbach.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4152" data-file-height="6356" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>21 October 1556
</td>
<td>The influential Italian author and <a href="/wiki/Libertine" title="Libertine">libertine</a> Pietro Aretino is said to have died of suffocation from <a href="/wiki/Death_from_laughter" title="Death from laughter">laughing too much</a> at an obscene joke during a meal in <a href="/wiki/Venice" title="Venice">Venice</a>. Another version states that he fell from a chair from too much laughter, fracturing his skull.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Hans Staininger
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG" class="image"><img alt="Braunau am Inn 003.JPG" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG/100px-Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG" decoding="async" width="100" height="133" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG/150px-Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG/200px-Braunau_am_Inn_003.JPG 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="1200" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1567
</td>
<td>Hans Staininger, the <a href="/wiki/Burgomaster" title="Burgomaster">burgomaster</a> of <a href="/wiki/Braunau_am_Inn" title="Braunau am Inn">Braunau</a> (then <a href="/wiki/Bavaria" title="Bavaria">Bavaria</a>, now <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austria</a>), died when he broke his neck by tripping over his own beard.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> The beard, which was 4.5 feet (1.4&#160;m) long at the time, was usually kept rolled up in a leather pouch.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Marco_Antonio_Bragadin" title="Marco Antonio Bragadin">Marco Antonio Bragadin</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Брагадино.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg/100px-%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="129" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg/150px-%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg/200px-%D0%91%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE.jpg 2x" data-file-width="276" data-file-height="356" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>17 August 1571
</td>
<td>Marco Antonio Bragadin, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Venice" title="Republic of Venice">Venetian</a> Captain-General of <a href="/wiki/Famagusta" title="Famagusta">Famagusta</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>, was gruesomely killed in August 1571 after the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottomans</a> took the city. He was dragged round the walls with sacks of earth and stone on his back; next, he was tied to a chair and hoisted to the yardarm of the Turkish flagship, where he was exposed to the taunts of the sailors. Finally, he was taken to his place of execution in the main square, tied naked to a column, and <a href="/wiki/Flaying" title="Flaying">flayed alive</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> Bragadin's skin was stuffed with straw and sewn, reinvested with his military insignia, and exhibited riding an ox in a mocking procession along the streets of Famagusta. The macabre trophy was hoisted upon the masthead pennant of the personal galley of the Ottoman commander, Amir al-bahr Mustafa Pasha, to be brought to <a href="/wiki/Constantinople" title="Constantinople">Constantinople</a> as a gift for <a href="/wiki/List_of_sultans_of_the_Ottoman_Empire" title="List of sultans of the Ottoman Empire">Sultan</a> <a href="/wiki/Selim_II" title="Selim II">Selim II</a>. Bragadin's skin was stolen in 1580 by a Venetian seaman and brought back to Venice, where it was received as a returning hero.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Tycho_Brahe" title="Tycho Brahe">Tycho Brahe</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Tycho_Brahe.JPG" class="image"><img alt="Tycho Brahe.JPG" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Tycho_Brahe.JPG/100px-Tycho_Brahe.JPG" decoding="async" width="100" height="148" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Tycho_Brahe.JPG/150px-Tycho_Brahe.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Tycho_Brahe.JPG/200px-Tycho_Brahe.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1081" data-file-height="1600" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>24 October 1601
</td>
<td>Tycho Brahe contracted a bladder or kidney ailment after attending a banquet in Prague, and died eleven days later. According to <a href="/wiki/Johannes_Kepler" title="Johannes Kepler">Kepler</a>'s first-hand account, Brahe had refused to leave the banquet to relieve himself because it would have been a breach of etiquette.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> After he had returned home he was no longer able to urinate, except eventually in very small quantities and with excruciating pain.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_modern_period">Early modern period</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Early modern period">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col">Name of person
</th>
<th scope="col">Image
</th>
<th scope="col">Date of death
</th>
<th scope="col">Details
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Thomas_Urquhart" title="Thomas Urquhart">Thomas Urquhart</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:ThomasUrquhart.png" class="image"><img alt="ThomasUrquhart.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/ThomasUrquhart.png/100px-ThomasUrquhart.png" decoding="async" width="100" height="148" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/ThomasUrquhart.png/150px-ThomasUrquhart.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/ThomasUrquhart.png/200px-ThomasUrquhart.png 2x" data-file-width="221" data-file-height="327" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1660
</td>
<td>Thomas Urquhart, a <a href="/wiki/Scottish_people" title="Scottish people">Scottish</a> aristocrat, <a href="/wiki/Polymath" title="Polymath">polymath</a> and first translator of <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Rabelais" title="François Rabelais">François Rabelais</a>'s writings into English, is said to have died laughing upon hearing that <a href="/wiki/Charles_II_of_England" title="Charles II of England">Charles II</a> had taken the throne.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">James Betts
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1667
</td>
<td>James Betts died from <a href="/wiki/Asphyxiation" class="mw-redirect" title="Asphyxiation">asphyxiation</a> after being sealed in a <a href="/wiki/Cupboard" title="Cupboard">cupboard</a> by Elizabeth Spencer, at <a href="/wiki/Corpus_Christi_College,_Cambridge" title="Corpus Christi College, Cambridge">Corpus Christi College, Cambridge</a> in an attempt to hide him from her father, <a href="/wiki/John_Spencer_(Master_of_Corpus_Christi_College,_Cambridge)" class="mw-redirect" title="John Spencer (Master of Corpus Christi College, Cambridge)">John Spencer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rackham_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rackham-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel" title="François Vatel">François Vatel</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Le suicide de François Vatel.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg/100px-Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="131" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg/150px-Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg/199px-Le_suicide_de_Fran%C3%A7ois_Vatel.jpg 2x" data-file-width="248" data-file-height="326" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>24 April 1671
</td>
<td>Vatel, the <a href="/wiki/Majordomo" title="Majordomo">majordomo</a> of <a href="/wiki/Louis,_Grand_Cond%C3%A9" title="Louis, Grand Condé">Prince Louis II de Bourbon-Condè</a>, was responsible for a banquet for 2,000 people hosted in honour of <a href="/wiki/Louis_XIV_of_France" title="Louis XIV of France">King Louis XIV</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Ch%C3%A2teau_de_Chantilly" title="Château de Chantilly">Château de Chantilly</a>, where he died. According to a letter by <a href="/wiki/Marie_de_Rabutin-Chantal,_marquise_de_S%C3%A9vign%C3%A9" title="Marie de Rabutin-Chantal, marquise de Sévigné">Madame de Sévigné</a>, Vatel was so distraught about the lateness of the seafood delivery and about other mishaps that he committed suicide with his sword, and his body was discovered when someone came to tell him of the arrival of the fish.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Moli%C3%A8re" title="Molière">Molière</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_(1622-1673)_-_Google_Art_Project_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Pierre Mignard - Portrait de Jean-Baptiste Poquelin dit Molière (1622-1673) - Google Art Project (cropped).jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_%281622-1673%29_-_Google_Art_Project_%28cropped%29.jpg/100px-Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_%281622-1673%29_-_Google_Art_Project_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="113" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_%281622-1673%29_-_Google_Art_Project_%28cropped%29.jpg/150px-Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_%281622-1673%29_-_Google_Art_Project_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_%281622-1673%29_-_Google_Art_Project_%28cropped%29.jpg/200px-Pierre_Mignard_-_Portrait_de_Jean-Baptiste_Poquelin_dit_Moli%C3%A8re_%281622-1673%29_-_Google_Art_Project_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3716" data-file-height="4214" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>17 February 1673<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</td>
<td>The French playwright Molière suffered a <a href="/wiki/Pulmonary_hemorrhage" title="Pulmonary hemorrhage">pulmonary hemorrhage</a> caused by <a href="/wiki/Tuberculosis" title="Tuberculosis">tuberculosis</a> while playing the character Argan, a severe <a href="/wiki/Hypochondriasis" title="Hypochondriasis">hypochondriac</a>, in his own play <i><a href="/wiki/The_Imaginary_Invalid" title="The Imaginary Invalid">Le malade imaginaire</a></i> (<i>The Imaginary Invalid</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Walsh_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Walsh-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> He disguised his convulsion as part of his performance and finished out the show,<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> which included a scene in which the character he was playing faked his own death to find out how his wife really felt about him.<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> After the show, Molière's actual wife, who played the daughter of his character, realized that he really was ill<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> and carried him across the street to their house in the same chair he had pretended to die in as part of the performance.<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> He began coughing up blood and she sent for a priest to hear him renounce his acting career so he could be buried on sacred ground,<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> but Molière died before a sympathetic priest could be found.<sup id="cite_ref-Burke2008_91-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Burke2008-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Walsh_92-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Walsh-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Bhai_Mati_Das" title="Bhai Mati Das">Bhai Mati Das</a>
<p><a href="/wiki/Bhai_Sati_Das" title="Bhai Sati Das">Bhai Sati Das</a>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Bhai_Dayala" title="Bhai Dayala">Bhai Dayala</a>
</p>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Bhai Mati Das.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg/100px-Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="75" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg/150px-Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg/200px-Bhai_Mati_Das.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1675
</td>
<td>Bhai Mati Das, Bhai Sati Das and Bhai Dayala are revered as early <a href="/wiki/Sikhs" title="Sikhs">Sikh</a> <a href="/wiki/Martyr" title="Martyr">martyrs</a>. By order of the <a href="/wiki/Mughal_emperors" title="Mughal emperors">Mughal emperor</a> <a href="/wiki/Aurangzeb" title="Aurangzeb">Aurangzeb</a>, Bhai Mati Das was executed by being bound between two pillars and <a href="/wiki/Death_by_sawing" title="Death by sawing">sawn in half</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> while his younger brother Bhai Sati Das wrapped in cotton wool soaked in oil and set on fire<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> and Bhai Dayala was <a href="/wiki/Death_by_boiling" title="Death by boiling">boiled in a cauldron</a> full of water and roasted over a block of charcoal.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Jean-Baptiste_Lully" title="Jean-Baptiste Lully">Jean-Baptiste Lully</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Paul Mignard - Jean-Baptiste Lully.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg/100px-Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="120" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg/150px-Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg/200px-Paul_Mignard_-_Jean-Baptiste_Lully.jpg 2x" data-file-width="532" data-file-height="637" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>22 March 1687
</td>
<td>Jean-Baptiste Lully, the French composer, died of a <a href="/wiki/Gangrene" title="Gangrene">gangrenous</a> <a href="/wiki/Abscess" title="Abscess">abscess</a> after accidentally piercing his foot with a staff while he was vigorously conducting a <i><a href="/wiki/Te_Deum" title="Te Deum">Te Deum</a></i>. It was customary at that time to conduct by banging a staff on the floor.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> He refused to have his leg amputated so he could still dance.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Stanis%C5%82aw_Leszczy%C5%84ski" title="Stanisław Leszczyński">Stanisław Leszczyński</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Wypadek Leszczynski.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg/100px-Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="80" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg/150px-Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg/200px-Wypadek_Leszczynski.jpg 2x" data-file-width="424" data-file-height="340" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>23 February 1766
</td>
<td>The former King Stanisław I of Poland, father-in-law of <a href="/wiki/Louis_XV_of_France" title="Louis XV of France">Louis XV of France</a>, died in 1766, at the age of 88, as a result of serious burns: his silk attire caught fire from a spark while the King was snoozing near the fireplace in his <a href="/wiki/Ch%C3%A2teau_de_Lun%C3%A9ville" title="Château de Lunéville">palace in Lunéville</a> on 5 February. Leszczyński was badly burned when the servants rescued him after a while, but he died after many days of agony.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Adolf_Frederick,_King_of_Sweden" title="Adolf Frederick, King of Sweden">Adolf Frederick, King of Sweden</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick,_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Gustaf Lundberg - Portrait of Adolf Frederick, King of Sweden - WGA13779.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick%2C_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg/100px-Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick%2C_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="129" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick%2C_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg/150px-Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick%2C_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick%2C_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg/200px-Gustaf_Lundberg_-_Portrait_of_Adolf_Frederick%2C_King_of_Sweden_-_WGA13779.jpg 2x" data-file-width="968" data-file-height="1248" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>12 February 1771
</td>
<td>Adolf Frederick, King of Sweden, died of digestion problems on 12 February 1771 after having consumed a meal of lobster, caviar, sauerkraut, smoked herring, and champagne, topped off with 14 servings of his favourite dessert: <a href="/wiki/Semla" title="Semla">semla</a> served in a bowl of hot milk, called "hetvägg".<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> He is thus remembered by Swedish schoolchildren as "the king who ate himself to death."<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="19th_century">19th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 19th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>

</th>

</th>
<th scope="col">Details
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">William Snyder
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>11 January 1854
</td>
<td>William Snyder, a 13-year-old, died in <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a>, California, when a circus clown swung him around by his heels.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Archduchess_Mathilda_of_Austria" title="Archduchess Mathilda of Austria">Mathilda of Austria</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Matilde de Áustria-Teschen.5.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg/100px-Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="163" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg/150px-Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg/200px-Matilde_de_%C3%81ustria-Teschen.5.jpg 2x" data-file-width="432" data-file-height="704" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>6 June 1867
</td>
<td>Archduchess Mathilda of Austria, daughter of <a href="/wiki/Archduke_Albrecht,_Duke_of_Teschen" title="Archduke Albrecht, Duke of Teschen">Archduke Albrecht, Duke of Teschen</a>, died at the age of 18 in <a href="/wiki/Schloss_Hetzendorf" title="Schloss Hetzendorf">Schloss Hetzendorf</a>. She had put on a <a href="/wiki/Gauze" title="Gauze">gauze</a> dress to go to the theatre. Before leaving for the theatre, she wanted to smoke a cigarette but shortly thereafter her father, who had forbidden smoking, approached her, and she hid the cigarette behind her dress, immediately setting light to its very flammable material and giving her second and third-degree <a href="/wiki/Burn" title="Burn">burns</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Clement_Vallandigham" title="Clement Vallandigham">Clement Vallandigham</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Clement Vallandigham - Brady-Handy.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg/100px-Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="156" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg/150px-Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg/200px-Clement_Vallandigham_-_Brady-Handy.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2712" data-file-height="4232" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>17 June 1871
</td>
<td>Clement Vallandigham, a lawyer and <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a> politician defending a man accused of murder, accidentally shot himself and died while demonstrating how the victim might have accidentally shot himself. His client was cleared.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Henry Taylor
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>November 1872
</td>
<td>Henry Taylor, a pall bearer at <a href="/wiki/Kensal_Green_Cemetery" title="Kensal Green Cemetery">Kensal Green Cemetery</a> in London, tripped over a stone and stumbled as he was carrying a coffin.<sup id="cite_ref-Clay2013_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Clay2013-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> The other pall bearers let go of the coffin<sup id="cite_ref-Clay2013_107-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Clay2013-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> and it fell on top of Taylor, crushing him to death in front of all the mourners.<sup id="cite_ref-Clay2013_107-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Clay2013-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> The widow of the man in the coffin reportedly "nearly went into hysterics".<sup id="cite_ref-Clay2013_107-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Clay2013-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Sir_William_Payne-Gallwey,_2nd_Baronet" title="Sir William Payne-Gallwey, 2nd Baronet">Sir William Payne-Gallwey, 2nd Baronet</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>19 December 1881
</td>
<td>Sir William Payne-Gallwey, a former British <a href="/wiki/Member_of_Parliament_(United_Kingdom)" title="Member of Parliament (United Kingdom)">MP</a>, sustained "severe internal injuries" when he fell over and landed on a <a href="/wiki/Turnip" title="Turnip">turnip</a> while out hunting. He died a few days later.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Allan_Pinkerton" title="Allan Pinkerton">Allan Pinkerton</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Allan Pinkerton-retouch.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg/100px-Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="116" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg/150px-Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg/200px-Allan_Pinkerton-retouch.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1661" data-file-height="1933" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1 July 1884
</td>
<td>Allan Pinkerton, the founder of the <a href="/wiki/Pinkerton_Detective_Agency" class="mw-redirect" title="Pinkerton Detective Agency">Pinkerton Detective Agency</a>, was in <a href="/wiki/Chicago" title="Chicago">Chicago</a>, <a href="/wiki/Illinois" title="Illinois">Illinois</a> when he tripped on the pavement and severely bit on his tongue.<sup id="cite_ref-Lanis1949_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lanis1949-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> His tongue became infected with <a href="/wiki/Gangrene" title="Gangrene">gangrene</a>, ultimately leading to his death.<sup id="cite_ref-Lanis1949_110-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lanis1949-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Unknown
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>22 August 1888
</td>
<td>At around 8.30pm, a shower of <a href="/wiki/Meteorite" title="Meteorite">meteorite</a> pieces fell “like rain” on a village in <a href="/wiki/Sulaymaniyah" title="Sulaymaniyah">Sulaymaniyah</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> (then part of the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman Empire</a>). One man died from the impact of one of the pieces, while another was also hit but was left paralysed. Corroborated by several official sources, the man's death is considered the first (and, as of 2020, only) credible evidence of a person being killed by a meteorite.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Empress_Elisabeth_of_Austria" title="Empress Elisabeth of Austria">Empress Elisabeth of Austria</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Assassinato_luigi.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Assassinato luigi.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Assassinato_luigi.jpg/100px-Assassinato_luigi.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="68" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Assassinato_luigi.jpg/150px-Assassinato_luigi.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Assassinato_luigi.jpg/200px-Assassinato_luigi.jpg 2x" data-file-width="376" data-file-height="257" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>10 September 1898
</td>
<td>During a trip in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>, Empress Elisabeth of Austria was stabbed to death, with a thin file, by the Italian anarchist <a href="/wiki/Luigi_Lucheni" title="Luigi Lucheni">Luigi Lucheni</a>. The weapon pierced the victim's <a href="/wiki/Pericardium" title="Pericardium">pericardium</a>, and a <a href="/wiki/Lung" title="Lung">lung</a>. Because of the sharpness and thinness of the file the wound was very narrow and, due to pressure from Elisabeth's extremely tight corseting, which was usually sewn onto her, she did not notice what had happened (in fact she believed a simple passerby had hit her) and continued to walk for a while before collapsing.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="20th_century">20th century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 20th century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="1901_.E2.80.93_1960"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1901_–_1960">1901 – 1960</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 1901 – 1960">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<tr>
<th scope="row">Unknown
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>Early 1903
</td>
<td>An unnamed person was beaten to death with a <a href="/wiki/Bible" title="Bible">Bible</a> during a healing ceremony gone wrong in <a href="/wiki/Honolulu" title="Honolulu">Honolulu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> The victim was being treated for <a href="/wiki/Malaria" title="Malaria">malaria</a> when his family summoned a <a href="/wiki/Kahuna" title="Kahuna">Kahuna</a> who decided he was possessed by devils and tried to exorcise the demons;<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> the Kahuna was brought up on a charge of manslaughter.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Grigori_Rasputin" title="Grigori Rasputin">Grigori Rasputin</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Rasputin_PA.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Rasputin PA.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Rasputin_PA.jpg/76px-Rasputin_PA.jpg" decoding="async" width="76" height="100" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Rasputin_PA.jpg/114px-Rasputin_PA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Rasputin_PA.jpg/152px-Rasputin_PA.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2276" data-file-height="3000" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>30 December
<p>[<a href="/wiki/Old_Style_and_New_Style_dates" title="Old Style and New Style dates">O.S.</a> 17 December] 1916
</p>
</td>
<td>According to the Russian mystic's murderer himself, Prince <a href="/wiki/Felix_Yusupov" title="Felix Yusupov">Felix Yusupov</a>, Rasputin consumed tea, cakes, and wine which had been laced with <a href="/wiki/Cyanide" title="Cyanide">cyanide</a> but he did not appear to be affected by the poison. He was then shot once in the chest and believed to be dead but, after a while, he leapt up and attacked Yusupov, who freed himself and fled. Rasputin followed and made it into the courtyard before being shot again and collapsing into a snowbank. The conspirators then wrapped Rasputin's body and dropped it into the <a href="/wiki/Little_Nevka_River" title="Little Nevka River">Malaya Nevka River</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Twenty-one people
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg" class="image"><img alt="BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg/100px-BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="80" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg/150px-BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg/200px-BostonMolassesDisaster.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="2388" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>15 January 1919
</td>
<td>A large storage tank burst in <a href="/wiki/North_End,_Boston" title="North End, Boston">Boston's North End</a>, releasing a wave of <a href="/wiki/Molasses" title="Molasses">molasses</a> which killed 21 people and injured 150. This event was later dubbed the <a href="/wiki/Great_Molasses_Flood" title="Great Molasses Flood">Great Molasses Flood</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Smithsonian_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Smithsonian-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/George_Herbert,_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon" title="George Herbert, 5th Earl of Carnarvon">George Herbert, 5th Earl of Carnarvon</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:George_Herbert,_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon,_reading.jpg" class="image"><img alt="George Herbert, 5th Earl of Carnarvon, reading.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/George_Herbert%2C_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon%2C_reading.jpg/100px-George_Herbert%2C_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon%2C_reading.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="132" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/George_Herbert%2C_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon%2C_reading.jpg/150px-George_Herbert%2C_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon%2C_reading.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/George_Herbert%2C_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon%2C_reading.jpg/200px-George_Herbert%2C_5th_Earl_of_Carnarvon%2C_reading.jpg 2x" data-file-width="340" data-file-height="450" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>5 April 1923
</td>
<td>George Herbert, 5th Earl of Carnarvon, who financed <a href="/wiki/Howard_Carter" title="Howard Carter">Howard Carter</a>'s search for <a href="/wiki/Tutankhamun" title="Tutankhamun">Tutankhamun</a>, died after a mosquito bite, which he had cut while shaving, became infected. Some attributed his death to the so-called <a href="/wiki/Curse_of_the_pharaohs" title="Curse of the pharaohs">curse of the pharaohs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Frank_Hayes_(jockey)" title="Frank Hayes (jockey)">Frank Hayes</a>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Frank_Hayes_(jockey).jpg" class="image" title="Portrait of Frank Hayes"><img alt="Portrait of Frank Hayes" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Frank_Hayes_%28jockey%29.jpg/100px-Frank_Hayes_%28jockey%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="194" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Frank_Hayes_%28jockey%29.jpg/150px-Frank_Hayes_%28jockey%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Frank_Hayes_%28jockey%29.jpg/200px-Frank_Hayes_%28jockey%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="424" data-file-height="821" /></a>
</td>
<td>4 June 1924
</td>
<td>The only race Frank Hayes, a 35-year-old jockey of <a href="/wiki/Elmont,_New_York" title="Elmont, New York">Elmont, New York</a> ever won was when he was dead. Riding a horse, Sweet Kiss, Frank suffered a fatal heart attack mid-race and collapsed on the horse. Sweet Kiss managed to still win with Frank Hayes' body on it, meaning he technically won.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Thornton Jones
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1924
</td>
<td>Jones, a lawyer in <a href="/wiki/Bangor,_Gwynedd" title="Bangor, Gwynedd">Bangor</a>, Wales, woke up to find that he had his throat slit. Motioning for a paper and a pencil, he wrote: "I dreamt that I had done it. I awoke to find it true," and died 80 minutes later. He had slit his throat himself while unconscious.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> An inquest at Bangor delivered a verdict of "suicide while temporarily insane."<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Bobby_Leach" title="Bobby Leach">Bobby Leach</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg" class="image"><img alt="BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg/100px-BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="59" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg/150px-BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg/200px-BobbyLeachNiagaraFalls.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="376" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1926
</td>
<td>Bobby Leach, an American stunt performer, died after a botched amputation of the infected leg which he had broken after slipping on an orange peel.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Phillip McClean
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1926
</td>
<td>Phillip McClean, aged 16, and his brother were clubbing a <a href="/wiki/Cassowary" title="Cassowary">cassowary</a> on the family property in <a href="/wiki/Mossman,_Queensland" title="Mossman, Queensland">Mossman, Queensland</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> when the bird knocked him down, kicked him in the neck, and opened a large cut, leading to death from loss of blood.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Isadora_Duncan" title="Isadora Duncan">Isadora Duncan</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Isadora Duncan portrait.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg/100px-Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="152" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg/150px-Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg/200px-Isadora_Duncan_portrait.jpg 2x" data-file-width="910" data-file-height="1380" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>14 September 1927
</td>
<td>Isadora Duncan, a dancer, broke her neck when her long scarf caught on the wheel of a car in which she was a passenger.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Sherwood_Anderson" title="Sherwood Anderson">Sherwood Anderson</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Sherwood_Anderson_(1933)_(retouched).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Sherwood Anderson (1933) (retouched).jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Sherwood_Anderson_%281933%29_%28retouched%29.jpg/100px-Sherwood_Anderson_%281933%29_%28retouched%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="127" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Sherwood_Anderson_%281933%29_%28retouched%29.jpg/150px-Sherwood_Anderson_%281933%29_%28retouched%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Sherwood_Anderson_%281933%29_%28retouched%29.jpg/200px-Sherwood_Anderson_%281933%29_%28retouched%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1194" data-file-height="1516" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>8 March 1941
</td>
<td>Sherwood Anderson, an American writer, died after an accidentally swallowed toothpick had damaged his gastrointestinal tract, causing an infection which led to <a href="/wiki/Peritonitis" title="Peritonitis">peritonitis</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Gareth_Jones_(actor)" title="Gareth Jones (actor)">Gareth Jones</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1958
</td>
<td>Gareth Jones, an actor, died of a heart attack between scenes of a live television play, <i><a href="/wiki/Underground_(1958_TV_play)" title="Underground (1958 TV play)">Underground</a></i>. Other members of the cast improvised lines, such as "I'm sure if So‑and‑so were here he would say..." to compensate for Jones's absence. Coincidentally, Jones's character was supposed to die of a heart attack in a later scene of the play.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Murray2003_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Murray2003-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<tr>
<th scope="row">John A. Byrnes, Richard Leroy McKinley, and Richard C. Legg
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:US_AEC_SL-1.JPG" class="image"><img alt="US AEC SL-1.JPG" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/US_AEC_SL-1.JPG/100px-US_AEC_SL-1.JPG" decoding="async" width="100" height="73" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/US_AEC_SL-1.JPG/150px-US_AEC_SL-1.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/US_AEC_SL-1.JPG/200px-US_AEC_SL-1.JPG 2x" data-file-width="346" data-file-height="253" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1961
</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">U.S. Army</a> specialists John A. Byrnes and Richard Leroy McKinley and <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">Navy</a> electrician's mate Richard C. Legg were killed by a <a href="/wiki/Water_hammer" title="Water hammer">water hammer</a> explosion during maintenance on the <a href="/wiki/SL-1" title="SL-1">SL-1</a> nuclear reactor in Idaho.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Tucker_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tucker-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Nick_Piantanida" title="Nick Piantanida">Nick Piantanida</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1966
</td>
<td>Nick Piantanida, a skydiver, died four months after an attempt to break the record for the highest parachute jump; his suit had depressurized causing brain damage.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1970s">1970s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 1970s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col">Name of person
</th>
<th scope="col">Image
</th>
<th scope="col">Date of death
</th>
<th scope="col">Details
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Georgy_Dobrovolsky" title="Georgy Dobrovolsky">Georgy Dobrovolsky</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vladislav_Volkov" title="Vladislav Volkov">Vladislav Volkov</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Patsayev" title="Viktor Patsayev">Viktor Patsayev</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Soyuz_11_crew.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Soyuz 11 crew.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Soyuz_11_crew.jpg/100px-Soyuz_11_crew.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="54" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Soyuz_11_crew.jpg/150px-Soyuz_11_crew.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Soyuz_11_crew.jpg/200px-Soyuz_11_crew.jpg 2x" data-file-width="836" data-file-height="448" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1971
</td>
<td>Georgy Dobrovolsky, Vladislav Volkov, and Viktor Patsayev, Soviet cosmonauts, died when their <a href="/wiki/Soyuz_11" title="Soyuz 11">Soyuz-11</a> spacecraft depressurized during preparations for re-entry. These are the only known human deaths outside the Earth's atmosphere.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Basil Brown
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1974
</td>
<td>Basil Brown, a 48-year-old health food advocate from <a href="/wiki/Croydon" title="Croydon">Croydon</a>, England, died from liver damage after he consumed 70 million <a href="/wiki/International_unit" title="International unit">units</a> of Vitamin A and around 10 US gallons (38 litres) of <a href="/wiki/Carrot_juice" title="Carrot juice">carrot juice</a> over ten days, turning his skin bright yellow.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Alex Mitchell
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1975
</td>
<td>After watching the "<a href="/wiki/Kung_Fu_Kapers" title="Kung Fu Kapers">Kung Fu Kapers</a>" episode of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Goodies_(TV_series)" title="The Goodies (TV series)">The Goodies</a></i>, Alex Mitchell laughed continuously for 25 minutes and then fell dead on his sofa from heart failure due to what doctors discovered years later, via his granddaughter, of a genetic condition called <a href="/wiki/Long_QT_syndrome" title="Long QT syndrome">Long QT syndrome</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Tina Christopherson
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1977
</td>
<td>Tina Christopherson died when she fanatically <a href="/wiki/Water_intoxication" title="Water intoxication">drank 4 US gallons (15 litres) of water a day</a> to combat stomach cancer.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Pryce" title="Tom Pryce">Tom Pryce</a> and Frederick Jansen van Vuuren
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1977
</td>
<td>Tom Pryce, a driver in the <a href="/wiki/1977_South_African_Grand_Prix" title="1977 South African Grand Prix">1977 South African Grand Prix</a>, was killed alongside fire marshal Frederick Jansen Van Vuuren after being struck on the head by a <a href="/wiki/Fire_extinguisher" title="Fire extinguisher">fire extinguisher</a> when his car, travelling at 170 miles per hour (270&#160;km/h), hit Jansen Van Vuuren as he was running across the <a href="/wiki/Kyalami" title="Kyalami">Kyalami</a> race track to extinguish a burning car.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Kurt_G%C3%B6del" title="Kurt Gödel">Kurt Gödel</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Kurt gödel.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/42/Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg/100px-Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="127" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/42/Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg/150px-Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/42/Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg/200px-Kurt_g%C3%B6del.jpg 2x" data-file-width="212" data-file-height="270" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1978
</td>
<td>Kurt Gödel, an Austrian-American logician and mathematician, died of starvation when his wife was hospitalized. Gödel refused to eat food prepared by anyone else<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> as he was suffering from an obsessive fear of being poisoned.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Robert_Williams_(robot_fatality)" title="Robert Williams (robot fatality)">Robert Williams</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1979
</td>
<td>Robert Williams, a worker at a Ford Motor Co. plant, became the first person known to be killed by a robot<sup id="cite_ref-rlid_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rlid-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> when the arm of a factory robot struck him in the head.<sup id="cite_ref-a_157-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-a-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">John Bowen
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1979
</td>
<td>John Bowen, a 20-year-old from <a href="/wiki/Nashua,_New_Hampshire" title="Nashua, New Hampshire">Nashua, New Hampshire</a>, was killed at a half-time show at <a href="/wiki/Shea_Stadium" title="Shea Stadium">Shea Stadium</a> when a 40-pound (18&#160;kg) model plane shaped like a lawnmower crashed into the stands.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Gergen2008_159-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gergen2008-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1980s">1980s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 1980s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
