<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Boris_Sagal" title="Boris Sagal">Boris Sagal</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1981
</td>
<td>Boris Sagal, a Ukrainian-American film director, died while shooting the TV miniseries <i><a href="/wiki/World_War_III_(miniseries)" title="World War III (miniseries)">World War III</a></i> in <a href="/wiki/Portland,_Oregon" title="Portland, Oregon">Portland</a>, Oregon, after he walked into the <a href="/wiki/Tail_rotor" title="Tail rotor">tail rotor</a> blade of a helicopter and was partially <a href="/wiki/Decapitation" title="Decapitation">decapitated</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-nytsagal_160-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nytsagal-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-salon1_161-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-salon1-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> He died five hours later at a hospital in Portland.<sup id="cite_ref-nytsagal_160-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nytsagal-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">David Grundman
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>February 4, 1982
</td>
<td>David Grundman, <a href="/wiki/Cactus_plugging" class="mw-redirect" title="Cactus plugging">shooting at cacti</a> with his shotgun near <a href="/wiki/Lake_Pleasant_Regional_Park" title="Lake Pleasant Regional Park">Lake Pleasant</a>, Arizona, was crushed when a 4-foot (1.2&#160;m) limb of the cactus detached and fell on him.<sup id="cite_ref-salon1_161-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-salon1-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Michael Scaglione
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>April 15, 1982
</td>
<td>Scaglione died after smashing his golf club against a golf cart. The head broke off and impaled him in the throat, severing his jugular vein.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Vic_Morrow" title="Vic Morrow">Vic Morrow</a>, Myca Dinh Le and Renee Shin-Yi Chen
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Vic Morrow in 1971.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg/100px-Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="155" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg/150px-Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg/200px-Vic_Morrow_in_1971.jpg 2x" data-file-width="550" data-file-height="850" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>July 23, 1982
</td>
<td>In the early morning hours of July 23, 1982, Morrow and two child actors, seven-year-old Myca Dinh Le, and six-year-old Renee Shin-Yi Chen, were filming <i><a href="/wiki/Twilight_Zone:_The_Movie" title="Twilight Zone: The Movie">Twilight Zone: The Movie</a></i> in California. They were performing in a scene for the Vietnam sequence, in which their characters attempt to escape from a deserted Vietnamese village while pursued by a U.S. Army helicopter. The helicopter was hovering at approximately 24 feet (7.3 m) above them when the heat from special effect pyrotechnic explosions reportedly delaminated the rotor blades<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> and caused the helicopter to crash on top of them, killing all three instantly. Morrow and Le were decapitated and mutilated by the helicopter rotor blades, while Chen was crushed by a helicopter strut.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Tennessee_Williams" title="Tennessee Williams">Tennessee Williams</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Tennessee Williams NYWTS.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg/100px-Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="113" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg/150px-Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg/200px-Tennessee_Williams_NYWTS.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2046" data-file-height="2310" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1983
</td>
<td>Tennessee Williams, an American playwright, died after accidentally choking on a plastic bottle cap which he was using to ingest <a href="/wiki/Barbiturate" title="Barbiturate">barbiturates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> Reports at the time of his death indicated he had died applying <a href="/wiki/Eye_drop" title="Eye drop">eye drops</a> while holding the cap between his teeth, but this was corrected in the official medical examiner's report six months later.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Truls Hellevik
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1983
</td>
<td>Truls Hellevik, a Norwegian diver, <a href="/wiki/Byford_Dolphin#Diving_bell_accident" title="Byford Dolphin">was explosively dismembered</a> when accidentally exposed to an eight-<a href="/wiki/Atmosphere_(unit)" class="mw-redirect" title="Atmosphere (unit)">atmosphere</a> change in <a href="/wiki/Air_pressure" class="mw-redirect" title="Air pressure">air pressure</a> which instantaneously forced his body through a 60-centimetre-diameter (24&#160;in) opening.<sup id="cite_ref-pmid3381801_169-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pmid3381801-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AADreport_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AADreport-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Dick_Wertheim" title="Dick Wertheim">Dick Wertheim</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1983
</td>
<td>Dick Wertheim, a <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a> linesman, died after a ball struck him in the groin and he fell out of his chair.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Jimmy Ferrozzo
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1983
</td>
<td>Jimmy Ferrozzo, a bouncer at the <a href="/wiki/Condor_Club" title="Condor Club">Condor Club</a> in San Francisco, died while engaging in sexual intercourse with his girlfriend Theresa Hill on a <a href="/wiki/Grand_piano" class="mw-redirect" title="Grand piano">grand piano</a> that was lowered from the ceiling by a hydraulic motor. Ferrozzo accidentally activated the lifting mechanism which pinned him against the ceiling leading to his suffocation.<sup id="cite_ref-nyt_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nyt-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> Hill survived the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-nyt_174-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nyt-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Jon-Erik_Hexum" title="Jon-Erik Hexum">Jon-Erik Hexum</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Jon-Erik_arms.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Jon-Erik arms.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Jon-Erik_arms.jpg/100px-Jon-Erik_arms.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="66" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Jon-Erik_arms.jpg/150px-Jon-Erik_arms.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Jon-Erik_arms.jpg/200px-Jon-Erik_arms.jpg 2x" data-file-width="628" data-file-height="416" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>1984
</td>
<td>Jon-Erik Hexum, an American actor, died after playing a simulated <a href="/wiki/Russian_roulette" title="Russian roulette">Russian roulette</a> with a <a href="/wiki/.44_Magnum" title=".44 Magnum">.44 Magnum</a> pistol loaded with <a href="/wiki/Blank_(cartridge)" title="Blank (cartridge)">blanks</a>. The blanks contained paper <a href="/wiki/Wadding" title="Wadding">wadding</a> and when Hexum pulled the trigger against his temple, the wadding was propelled with a force that broke Hexum's skull, causing a massive <a href="/wiki/Intracerebral_hemorrhage" title="Intracerebral hemorrhage">brain bleeding</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Unknown
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1984
</td>
<td>An unidentified 25-year-old man was using submersion as an <a href="/wiki/Erotic_asphyxia" class="mw-redirect" title="Erotic asphyxia">erotic asphyxia</a> method. With a home-made plastic body suit, he tied himself to a boat and was using a home-made diving apparatus for air supply. He died from rebreathing, caused by the faulty air supply device.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Franco Brun
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1987
</td>
<td>Brun, 22, an inmate at the Metro <a href="/wiki/Toronto_East_Detention_Centre" title="Toronto East Detention Centre">Toronto East Detention Centre</a> in Canada, died trying to swallow a pocket-size bible.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Cachy the Poodle, Marta Espina, Edith Solá, unidentified man
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1988
</td>
<td>A <a href="/wiki/Poodle" title="Poodle">poodle</a> named Cachy, in <a href="/wiki/Caballito,_Buenos_Aires" title="Caballito, Buenos Aires">Caballito, Buenos Aires</a>, fell from 13 floors and fatally hit 75-year-old Marta Espina, killing both instantly. In the course of the events, 46-year-old Edith Sola, who came to see the incident, was fatally hit by a bus. An unidentified man, who witnessed Edith's death, had an heart attack and also died, on his way to the hospital.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Ivan Lester McGuire
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1988
</td>
<td>On Saturday, April 2, veteran <a href="/wiki/Parachuting" title="Parachuting">sky diver</a> Ivan Lester McGuire was filming a jump by an instructor and student from the Franklin County Sports Parachute Center when he jumped from a plane without a parachute.  Focused on the filming process, McGuire apparently forgot to put on a parachute, and his camera equipment may have been mistaken for a chute. The tape was recovered.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1990s">1990s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 1990s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<tr>
<th scope="row">Daniel John O'Brien
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>January 14, 1990
</td>
<td>Daniel John O'Brien, 31, committed suicide by jumping into the engines of a British Airways 747 Jumbo.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Brandon_Lee" title="Brandon Lee">Brandon Lee</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1993
</td>
<td>Brandon Lee, 28-year-old film actor, martial artist, and son of <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Lee" title="Bruce Lee">Bruce Lee</a>, was accidentally shot to death by co-star <a href="/wiki/Michael_Massee" title="Michael Massee">Michael Massee</a> while filming a scene for <i><a href="/wiki/The_Crow_(1994_film)" title="The Crow (1994 film)">The Crow</a></i>, as the result of an <a href="/wiki/Squib_load" title="Squib load">improperly-loaded</a> prop gun.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Garry_Hoy" class="mw-redirect" title="Garry Hoy">Garry Hoy</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1993
</td>
<td>Garry Hoy, a lawyer in <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a> fell to his death from the 24th floor of the <a href="/wiki/Toronto-Dominion_Centre" title="Toronto-Dominion Centre">Toronto-Dominion Centre</a> while demonstrating to a group of visitors that the building's windows were "unbreakable". Hoy threw himself against the window, which did not break but popped out of its frame.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Death_of_Gloria_Ramirez" title="Death of Gloria Ramirez">Gloria Ramirez</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1994
</td>
<td>Gloria Ramirez, 31, died from <a href="/wiki/Kidney_failure" title="Kidney failure">kidney failure</a> related to her <a href="/wiki/Cervical_cancer" title="Cervical cancer">cervical cancer</a>. While treating her, several of the hospital staff became ill, suffering from loss of consciousness, shortness of breath and muscle spasms. Shortly before dying, Ramirez was allegedly covered with an oily sheen, which smelled of fruit and garlic. When drawing her blood with a syringe, nurses noticed it had a smell similar to <a href="/wiki/Ammonia" title="Ammonia">ammonia</a> and there were unusual particles floating in it.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Karen_Wetterhahn" title="Karen Wetterhahn">Karen Wetterhahn</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1997
</td>
<td>Karen Wetterhahn, a professor of chemistry at <a href="/wiki/Dartmouth_College" title="Dartmouth College">Dartmouth College</a>, died ten months after a few drops of <a href="/wiki/Dimethylmercury" title="Dimethylmercury">dimethylmercury</a> (an <a href="/wiki/Organomercury_compound" class="mw-redirect" title="Organomercury compound">organomercury compound</a> and one of the strongest known <a href="/wiki/Neurotoxin" title="Neurotoxin">neurotoxins</a>)  landed on her protective gloves. Although Wetterhahn had been following the required procedures, the material permeated the gloves and her skin within seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Loback1997_193-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Loback1997-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Bena Tshadi (football team)
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>October 1998
</td>
<td>An entire <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> team of 11 in <a href="/wiki/Kasai-Oriental_(former_province)" title="Kasai-Oriental (former province)">Eastern Kasai</a>, Democratic Republic of the Congo, were fatally struck by lightning while playing. The other team left the scene unharmed.<sup id="cite_ref-AP-19981028_194-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AP-19981028-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Jonathan Capewell
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1998
</td>
<td>Jonathan Capewell, 16, died from a heart attack brought on by the buildup of <a href="/wiki/Butane" title="Butane">butane</a> and <a href="/wiki/Propane" title="Propane">propane</a> in the blood after excessive use of <a href="/wiki/Deodorant" title="Deodorant">deodorant</a> sprays.<sup id="cite_ref-capewell_195-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-capewell-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> Capewell was reported to have an obsession with personal hygiene.<sup id="cite_ref-capewell_195-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-capewell-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> An autopsy showed that Capewell had 0.37&#160;mg of butane per litre in his blood, and the same amount of propane, whereas 0.1&#160;mg per litre can be fatal.<sup id="cite_ref-capewell_195-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-capewell-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="21st_century">21st century</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 21st century">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2000s">2000s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2000s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<tr>
<th scope="row">Bernd Brandes
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>9 March 2001
</td>
<td>Bernd Brandes, a German <a href="/wiki/Engineer" title="Engineer">engineer</a> from Berlin, was willingly slaughtered so that he could be butchered and eaten by <a href="/wiki/Cannibalism" title="Cannibalism">cannibal</a> <a href="/wiki/Armin_Meiwes" title="Armin Meiwes">Armin Meiwes</a>. Brandes had responded to an internet advertisement which Meiwes had placed for this purpose. In prison, Meiwes became a vegetarian.<sup id="cite_ref-news0_196-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-news0-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Michael Colombini
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2001
</td>
<td>Michael Colombini, 6, died during a <a href="/wiki/Magnetic_resonance_imaging" title="Magnetic resonance imaging">MRI</a> scan, after an oxygen tank was magnetically pulled into the machine and fractured his skull.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Death_of_Brian_Wells" title="Death of Brian Wells">Brian Douglas Wells</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>28 August 2003
</td>
<td>Brian Douglas Wells, a pizza delivery man from <a href="/wiki/Erie,_Pennsylvania" title="Erie, Pennsylvania">Erie, Pennsylvania</a>, was killed by an explosive collar around his neck, as part of a bank-robbery scheme.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Hitoshi Nikaidoh
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2003
</td>
<td>Hitoshi Nikaidoh, a doctor in <a href="/wiki/Houston" title="Houston">Houston</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, was decapitated after his head was trapped in the doors of an elevator at his workplace.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Phillip Quinn
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2004
</td>
<td>Phillip Quinn, 24, from <a href="/wiki/Kent,_Washington" title="Kent, Washington">Kent</a>, Washington, was killed when a <a href="/wiki/Lava_lamp" title="Lava lamp">lava lamp</a> he was heating on a stove exploded and a shard pierced his heart.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Enumclaw_horse_sex_case" title="Enumclaw horse sex case">Kenneth Pinyan</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2005
</td>
<td>Kenneth Pinyan died from injuries caused by <a href="/wiki/Anal_sex" title="Anal sex">anal sex</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Stallion" title="Stallion">stallion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Mildred Bowman and Alice Wardle
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2005
</td>
<td>Mildred Bowman, 62, and Alice Wardle, 68, were two sisters killed in <a href="/wiki/Benidorm" title="Benidorm">Benidorm</a>, Spain after becoming trapped for four days when their fold-up bed collapsed.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Steve_Irwin" title="Steve Irwin">Steve Irwin</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Steve_Irwin.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Steve Irwin.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Steve_Irwin.jpg/100px-Steve_Irwin.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="84" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Steve_Irwin.jpg/150px-Steve_Irwin.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Steve_Irwin.jpg/200px-Steve_Irwin.jpg 2x" data-file-width="982" data-file-height="820" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>4 September 2006
</td>
<td>Steve Irwin was a world-renowned Australian wildlife expert and television personality best known for his wildlife documentary show <i><a href="/wiki/The_Crocodile_Hunter" title="The Crocodile Hunter">The Crocodile Hunter</a></i>, and was well known for often handling and interacting with dangerous, often predatory animals such as crocodiles and venomous snakes. Irwin died from blood loss after being pierced in the heart by a startled <a href="/wiki/Short-tail_stingray" title="Short-tail stingray">short-tail stingray</a>'s barb while filming in shallow water in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Barrier_Reef" title="Great Barrier Reef">Great Barrier Reef</a> for <a href="/wiki/Bindi_the_Jungle_Girl" title="Bindi the Jungle Girl">his daughter's television program</a> during a lull in filming for <i><a href="/wiki/Ocean%27s_Deadliest" title="Ocean&#39;s Deadliest">Ocean's Deadliest</a></i>, another wildlife documentary series Irwin was taking part in. Unlike many of the animals Irwin gained fame and notoriety for interacting with, stingrays were not often viewed as particularly dangerous animals by many prior to this incident. The incident was captured on film, and it was considered the only known video recording of a fatality by a stingray. The footage was never released, and all recordings of the incident were destroyed at the behest of Irwin's family.<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Humberto Hernandez
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2007
</td>
<td>Humberto Hernandez, a 24-year-old <a href="/wiki/Oakland,_California" title="Oakland, California">Oakland</a>, California resident, was killed after being struck in the face by an airborne <a href="/wiki/Fire_hydrant" title="Fire hydrant">fire hydrant</a> while walking. A passing car had struck the fire hydrant and the water pressure shot the hydrant at Hernandez with enough force to kill him.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Harris2007_208-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Harris2007-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Adelir_Ant%C3%B4nio_de_Carli" title="Adelir Antônio de Carli">Adelir Antônio de Carli</a> aka <b>Padre Baloeiro</b> or <b>Padre do Balão</b>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>21 April 2008
</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Adelir_Ant%C3%B4nio_de_Carli" title="Adelir Antônio de Carli">Adelir Antônio de Carli</a>, also known in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> as Padre Baloeiro or Padre do Balão ("Balloon Priest" in Portuguese), was a Brazilian Catholic priest and <a href="/wiki/Skydiver" class="mw-redirect" title="Skydiver">skydiver</a> from <a href="/wiki/Pelotas" title="Pelotas">Pelotas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rio_Grande_do_Sul" title="Rio Grande do Sul">Rio Grande do Sul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, who on April 20, 2008, participated in a fundraising charity event for the Pastoral Rodoviária de Paranaguá (a religious entity that provides assistance to road travelers). For that he wanted to break a record of an American who had flown for 19 hours. Then fully equipped and with a total of 1000 balloons he flew to beat the record, reaching an altitude of 6,000 meters (or 19,700 ft). However, his balloon flight started to go wrong, and the priest ended up losing contact with the authorities (his last contact being with the military police near <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Francisco_do_Sul" title="São Francisco do Sul">São Francisco do Sul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Santa_Catarina" class="mw-disambig" title="Santa Catarina">Santa Catarina</a>, Brazil). Two months later, on <a href="/wiki/July_4" title="July 4">July 4</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic Ocean</a>, the members of an oil extraction vessel 100km from <a href="/wiki/Maca%C3%A9" title="Macaé">Macaé</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro_(state)" title="Rio de Janeiro (state)">Rio de Janeiro</a> find the lower part of a body, which appeared to be that of a male person. On July 29, DNA tests were done with the help of the priest's brother and his DNA. To the shock of the parish and the Brazilian population, the lower part of the body belonged to Padre do Balão. His death was so strange and unusual that he was "awarded" with a <a href="/wiki/Darwin_Awards" title="Darwin Awards">Darwin Awards</a> (the prize that is given to people who had the strangest and/or idiotic deaths and who were considered unusual deaths).<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Carlos_Alhinho" title="Carlos Alhinho">Carlos Alhinho</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>31 May 2008
</td>
<td>Carlos Alhinho, 59-year-old Portuguese professional football central defender and manager, died in <a href="/wiki/Benguela" title="Benguela">Benguela</a>, Angola after he opened the doors of a elevator and stepped in, only to find the carriage was not there but on the ground floor. He fell five floors onto the top of the cabin, and, though receiving immediate medical attention, died shortly afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>

</td>
<td>The two young brothers, aged 4 and 6, were <a href="/wiki/2013_New_Brunswick_python_attack" title="2013 New Brunswick python attack">killed by an African rock python</a> during a sleepover at their friend's home in <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick" title="New Brunswick">New Brunswick</a>, Canada. The large snake had escaped its enclosure in the apartment and slithered through ducts until it fell through the ceiling of the bedroom where they slept. Though it suffocated the children it did not attempt to eat them.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup>

Yıldırım's father placed the goat on the roof of the building where he lived because he could not find another suitable place to keep it.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup>

<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Christophe_de_Margerie" title="Christophe de Margerie">Christophe de Margerie</a>

<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_(besoindair)_2009-09-04.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Christophe Jacquin de Margerie (besoindair) 2009-09-04.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_%28besoindair%29_2009-09-04.jpg/100px-Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_%28besoindair%29_2009-09-04.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="150" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_%28besoindair%29_2009-09-04.jpg/150px-Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_%28besoindair%29_2009-09-04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_%28besoindair%29_2009-09-04.jpg/200px-Christophe_Jacquin_de_Margerie_%28besoindair%29_2009-09-04.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3744" data-file-height="5616" /></a></div></div>

<td>20 October 2014

<td>Christophe de Margerie, an oil executive, was killed when his corporate jet collided with a snowplow reportedly driven by a drunk driver.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup>

<th scope="row">V. Kamaraj
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2016
</td>
<td>V. Kamaraj, a 40-year-old Indian bus driver, was claimed by local <a href="/wiki/List_of_newspapers_in_India" title="List of newspapers in India">Indian newspapers</a> to have been killed by a <a href="/wiki/Meteorite" title="Meteorite">meteorite</a> which left a two-foot (61&#160;cm) crater, although officials from NASA oppose that view saying that the most likely explanation was a land-based explosion. According to a preliminary report by the National College Instrumentation Facility (NCIF) in <a href="/wiki/Tiruchirappalli" title="Tiruchirappalli">Trichy</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Scanning_electron_microscope" title="Scanning electron microscope">scanning electron microscope</a> (SEM) study on the evidence of the samples retrieved from the campus in <a href="/wiki/Vellore" title="Vellore">Vellore</a> from where the blast occurred showed "the presence of <a href="/wiki/Carbonaceous_Chondrite" class="mw-redirect" title="Carbonaceous Chondrite">carbonaceous chondrites</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;273&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">&#91;274&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">&#91;275&#93;</a></sup>

<th scope="row">Kristopher Moules and Timothy Gilliam Jr.
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2016
</td>
<td>Kristopher Moules, 25, a Corrections Officer and Timothy Gilliam Jr., 27, an out of county inmate being housed at the Luzerne County Correctional Facility in <a href="/wiki/Luzerne_County,_Pennsylvania" title="Luzerne County, Pennsylvania">Luzerne County</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</a>, fell to their deaths after an altercation between the two caused them to slam into the exterior of the fifth floor elevator doors. Despite the elevator having its up-to-date working credentials, upon impact of the men into the elevator doors, the doors popped open, causing the two men to fall five flights down the elevator shaft to their deaths. The county declared CO Moules’ death a homicide and declared Gilliam’ death an accident.<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">&#91;286&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>

<th scope="row">Ten people
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2016
</td>
<td>On 21 November 2016, a powerful <a href="/wiki/Southerly_buster" class="mw-redirect" title="Southerly buster">southerly change</a> in <a href="/wiki/Melbourne" title="Melbourne">Melbourne</a>, Australia, resulted in the death of 10 <a href="/wiki/Asthmatic" class="mw-redirect" title="Asthmatic">asthmatic</a> people who succumbed to <a href="/wiki/Respiratory_failure" title="Respiratory failure">respiratory failure</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">&#91;287&#93;</a></sup> This was due to a stark wind (60&#160;km/hour) that distributed <a href="/wiki/Ryegrass" class="mw-redirect" title="Ryegrass">ryegrass</a> <a href="/wiki/Pollen" title="Pollen">pollen</a> into the moist air, rupturing them into very fine specks, small enough particles to enter people's lungs.<sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup>

<th scope="row">Elizabeth Isherwood
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2017
</td>
<td>Elizabeth Isherwood, 60, walked naked into an airing cupboard at the villa she was renting and shut the door. When she tried to leave, part of the door handle broke off in her hand. She dug into the wall in an attempt to escape, but struck and burst a pipe, which sprayed water into the cupboard and caused her eventual death by <a href="/wiki/Hypothermia" title="Hypothermia">hypothermia</a>. She was found several days later. Why she had shut herself in the cupboard in the first place remained a mystery.<sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">&#91;296&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Rajesh Maru
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2018
</td>
<td>Rajesh Maru, 32, died at Nair Hospital in <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Mumbai</a> after carrying a metal <a href="/wiki/Oxygen_tank" title="Oxygen tank">oxygen tank</a> into a room housing an <a href="/wiki/MRI_scanner" class="mw-redirect" title="MRI scanner">MRI scanner</a>; the machine's <a href="/wiki/Magnetic_field" title="Magnetic field">magnetic field</a> pulled Maru in, pinning his hand and breaching the tank, releasing <a href="/wiki/Liquid_oxygen" title="Liquid oxygen">liquid oxygen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-week_297-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-week-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup> A hospital employee had asked Maru to transport the tank, as Maru's hospitalized relative would need it during her scan.<sup id="cite_ref-week_297-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-week-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-298" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-298">&#91;298&#93;</a></sup> An autopsy showed that Maru died instantly from <a href="/wiki/Pneumothorax" title="Pneumothorax">pneumothorax</a> brought on by exposure to very high levels of leaked oxygen.<sup id="cite_ref-week_297-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-week-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup> Conflicting reports state two or three hospital employees were arrested for <a href="/wiki/Negligence" title="Negligence">negligence</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_299-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-299">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-week_297-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-week-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Maharashtra" title="Maharashtra">Maharashtra</a> state government compensated Maru's family 500,000 <a href="/wiki/Indian_rupee" title="Indian rupee">rupees</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_299-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-299">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>

<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Death_of_Elaine_Herzberg" title="Death of Elaine Herzberg">Elaine Herzberg</a>
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2018
</td>
<td>Elaine Herzberg, a 49-year-old woman in <a href="/wiki/Tempe,_Arizona" title="Tempe, Arizona">Tempe, Arizona</a>, died after being hit by a <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_car" class="mw-redirect" title="Autonomous car">self-driving car</a> operated by <a href="/wiki/Uber" title="Uber">Uber</a>, as she crossed the road, in what was reported to be the first death of a pedestrian struck by a self-driving car on public roads. In response to the fatal accident, Uber suspended self-driving car tests in all U.S. cities.<sup id="cite_ref-300" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-300">&#91;300&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301">&#91;301&#93;</a></sup>

<th scope="row">Kyle Plush
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>10 April 2018
</td>
<td>On 10 April 2018, 16-year-old high-school student Kyle Plush died after becoming trapped in his <a href="/wiki/Honda_Odyssey_(North_America)" title="Honda Odyssey (North America)">Honda Odyssey</a>, which was in his school's parking lot in <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati" title="Cincinnati">Cincinnati</a>, Ohio.  Attempting to reach his tennis equipment, Plush leaned over the third row of seats into the trunk.  When the row of seats "squashed his chest", Plush became pinned and later died.  During the incident, the teen called 9-1-1 twice, by using <a href="/wiki/IPhone" title="IPhone">Apple iPhone</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Siri" title="Siri">Siri</a> voice-activation.  Responding to the 9-1-1 calls, police were not able to find Plush; he was eventually discovered in the vehicle by his father about six hours later.<sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303">&#91;303&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>

<td>2018

She was partially sucked out through the window, but was pulled back into the aircraft and was given <a href="/wiki/CPR" class="mw-redirect" title="CPR">CPR</a> until an <a href="/wiki/Emergency_landing" title="Emergency landing">emergency landing</a> was made. She died upon arrival at hospital with her cause of death determined to be <a href="/wiki/Blunt_trauma" title="Blunt trauma">blunt trauma</a> to the head, neck and torso.<sup id="cite_ref-304" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-304">&#91;304&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-305" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-305">&#91;305&#93;</a></sup>

</td>
<td>Linda Goldbloom, 79, died after being hit by a <a href="/wiki/Foul_ball" title="Foul ball">foul ball</a> at <a href="/wiki/Dodger_Stadium" title="Dodger Stadium">Dodger Stadium</a>. Goldbloom's death was the first in nearly 50 years directly attributed to a foul ball.<sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310">&#91;310&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Salvator Disi
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>2019
</td>
<td>Salvator Disi, 62, was decapitated while using a <a href="/wiki/Ground_support_equipment#Ground_power_units" title="Ground support equipment">power cart</a> to <a href="/wiki/Jump_start_(vehicle)" title="Jump start (vehicle)">jump start</a> a helicopter in <a href="/wiki/Hernando_County,_Florida" title="Hernando County, Florida">Hernando County, Florida</a>. The unexpected up-and-down motion of the helicopter caused the <a href="/wiki/Rotor_blade" class="mw-redirect" title="Rotor blade">rotor blades</a> to strike Disi.<sup id="cite_ref-311" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-311">&#91;311&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Darren Hickey
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>5 April 2019
</td>
<td>On 5 April 2019, Darren Hickey, a 51-year-old <a href="/wiki/Wedding_planner" title="Wedding planner">wedding planner</a> from <a href="/wiki/Horwich" title="Horwich">Horwich</a>, England, died after eating a scalding-hot <a href="/wiki/Fishcake" title="Fishcake">fishcake</a> at a wedding.  The cause of death was ruled to be <a href="/wiki/Asphyxia" title="Asphyxia">asphyxiation</a>.  The <a href="/wiki/Pathology" title="Pathology">pathologist</a> who performed Hickey's <a href="/wiki/Autopsy" title="Autopsy">autopsy</a> called the case "extremely rare" and likened Hickey's symptoms to those of victims who have inhaled smoke during house fires.<sup id="cite_ref-312" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-312">&#91;312&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Paul McDonald
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>17 April 2019
</td>
<td>Paul McDonald, 47, was attacked and killed by a pet <a href="/wiki/Deer" title="Deer">deer</a> on his property in north-east <a href="/wiki/Victoria_(Australia)" title="Victoria (Australia)">Victoria, Australia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-313" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-313">&#91;313&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-314" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-314">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Elena Struthers-Gardner
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>July 2019
</td>
<td>Elena "Lena" Struthers-Gardner, 60, was carrying a mason-jar style drinking glass with a screw-top lid in her kitchen when she collapsed. The 10-inch stainless steel straw entered her left eye socket and pierced her brain.<sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315">&#91;315&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-316" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-316">&#91;316&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Yulia Sharkom
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>8 September 2019
</td>
<td>Yulia Sharkom, 21, was trying to grab her 2-year-old daughter from her car through the half-open front seat window in <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> when her neck was jammed by the window after her daughter pressed the automatic switch. She died eight days later, having suffered <a href="/wiki/Asphyxia" title="Asphyxia">asphyxia</a> leading to <a href="/wiki/Brain_damage" title="Brain damage">brain damage</a> due to the accidental window <a href="/wiki/Garrote" title="Garrote">garroting</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-317" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-317">&#91;317&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Michael Kosanovich
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>6 December 2019
</td>
<td>Michael Kosanovich, 21, was crushed to death by a 2002 Lexus IS300s automobile after its owner started it by remote control. The car rolled forward, and he was pinned between two vehicles.<sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318">&#91;318&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319">&#91;319&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2020s">2020s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2020s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col">Name of person
</th>
<th scope="col">Image
</th>
<th scope="col">Date of death
</th>
<th scope="col">Details
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th>Sergio Millán
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>14 January 2020
</td>
<td>Sergio Millán, 59, was killed when the ceiling of his flat in Torreforta, Tarragona (Spain) collapsed on him. The collapse was caused by a heavy metal plate that flew 3&#160;km propelled by an explosion from a factory in the outskirts of the town and eventually crashed into the flat.<sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320">&#91;320&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (February 2020)">clarification needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Hoong Leong
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>18 February 2020
</td>
<td>Hoong Leong, 37, was struck in the shoulder by a falling <a href="/wiki/Gas_cylinder" title="Gas cylinder">gas cylinder</a> whilst walking home during <a href="/wiki/Severe_storm_events_in_Sydney" title="Severe storm events in Sydney">stormy conditions</a> near <a href="/wiki/The_Rocks,_New_South_Wales" title="The Rocks, New South Wales">The Rocks</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sydney,_Australia" class="mw-redirect" title="Sydney, Australia">Sydney, Australia</a>. Leong survived the initial impact but went into <a href="/wiki/Cardiac_arrest" title="Cardiac arrest">cardiac arrest</a> and died upon arrival at hospital.<sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321">&#91;321&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-322" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-322">&#91;322&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Valentin Didenko, Yury Alferov, Natalia Monakova
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>29 February 2020
</td>
<td>Three people died of <a href="/wiki/Hypercapnia" title="Hypercapnia">carbon dioxide suffocation</a> and <a href="/wiki/Drowning" title="Drowning">drowning</a> when 25 kg of <a href="/wiki/Dry_ice" title="Dry ice">dry ice</a> was thrown into an indoors swimming pool at a sauna party in Moscow to create a layer of thick white fog over water surface, which, inadvertently, displaced <a href="/wiki/Oxygen" title="Oxygen">oxygen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-323" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-323">&#91;323&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-324" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-324">&#91;324&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-325" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-325">&#91;325&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/Stanislav_Bogdanovich" title="Stanislav Bogdanovich">Stanislav Bogdanovich</a> and Alexandra Vernigora
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Stanislav Bogdanovich 2014.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg/100px-Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="125" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg/150px-Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg/200px-Stanislav_Bogdanovich_2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2400" data-file-height="3000" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>5 March 2020
</td>
<td>Bogdanovich was found dead on 5 March 2020 in his <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> apartment, alongside <a href="/wiki/Nitrous_oxide" title="Nitrous oxide">nitrous oxide</a>-filled balloons and the body of his girlfriend, Alexandra Vernigora, also a chess player. Police do not suspect foul play.<sup id="cite_ref-326" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-326">&#91;326&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327">&#91;327&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Paulynho Paixão
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>3 April 2020
</td>
<td>Paulynho Paixão (Real Name: Francisco de Paula Moura), 43 was one of the most famous singers in <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Brazil" class="mw-redirect" title="Northeast Brazil">Northeast Brazil</a>. However, on April 3 he was the victim of a fatal accident with strange circumstances: he died after suffering two accidents in an interval of three hours. Paulynho Paixão hours earlier, on Thursday (April 2nd) he had survived the first accident (a car accident), near the city of <a href="/wiki/Passagem_Franca_do_Piau%C3%AD" title="Passagem Franca do Piauí">Passagem Franca do Piauí</a>, <a href="/wiki/Piaui" class="mw-redirect" title="Piaui">Piaui</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> leaving without injuries. However, three hours later (dawn on Friday, April 3rd) Paulynho Paixão went to the place of the first accident to try to recover the crashed car, but ended up suffering a second accident (a motorcycle accident, the most fatal one) that ended up killing him on the spot (at the <b>same</b> location as the car accident <b>three hours before</b>). Due to the mysterious circumstances of the motorcycle accident that killed him, investigations are ongoing.<sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328">&#91;328&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-329" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-329">&#91;329&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-330" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-330">&#91;330&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-331" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-331">&#91;331&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Animal_deaths">Animal deaths</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Animal deaths">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Expand_section plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="image"><img alt="[icon]" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs expansion</b>. <small>You can help by <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_unusual_deaths&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.</small>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">November 2019</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>This section is for the deaths of animals, for whom there are several sources mentioning the deaths as unusual.
</p>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th scope="col">Name of animal
</th>
<th scope="col">Image
</th>
<th scope="col">Date of death
</th>
<th scope="col">Details
</th></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Three cows, three sheep, two sows
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>1662
</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Cotton_Mather" title="Cotton Mather">Cotton Mather</a> writes how one William Potter was hanged for bestiality, as were the animals involved.<sup id="cite_ref-332" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-332">&#91;332&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-333" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-333">&#91;333&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Topsy_(elephant)" title="Topsy (elephant)">Topsy the elephant</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Topsy_the_elephant.png" class="image"><img alt="Topsy the elephant.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Topsy_the_elephant.png/100px-Topsy_the_elephant.png" decoding="async" width="100" height="105" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Topsy_the_elephant.png/150px-Topsy_the_elephant.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Topsy_the_elephant.png/200px-Topsy_the_elephant.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="836" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>4 January 1903
</td>
<td>Topsy was executed by poisoning, electrocution, and strangulation. A <a href="/wiki/Electrocuting_an_Elephant" title="Electrocuting an Elephant">74-second film</a> of the electrocution was recorded and preserved. It may have been the first time death was ever captured in a motion picture film.<sup id="cite_ref-334" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-334">&#91;334&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint noexcerpt Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTRS" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NOTRS"><span title="This claim needs references to better sources. (April 2018)">better&#160;source&#160;needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Mary_(elephant)" title="Mary (elephant)">Mary the elephant</a>
</th>
<td><div class="center"><div class="floatnone"><a href="/wiki/File:Elephantmary.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Elephantmary.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Elephantmary.jpg/100px-Elephantmary.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="139" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Elephantmary.jpg/150px-Elephantmary.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Elephantmary.jpg/200px-Elephantmary.jpg 2x" data-file-width="365" data-file-height="509" /></a></div></div>
</td>
<td>13 September 1916
</td>
<td>The day after <a href="/wiki/Mary_(elephant)" title="Mary (elephant)">Mary</a>, a five-ton cow elephant, killed a trainer for the <i>Sparks World Famous Shows</i> circus in <a href="/wiki/Sullivan_County,_Tennessee" title="Sullivan County, Tennessee">Sullivan County</a>, Tennessee, she was <a href="/wiki/Hanged" class="mw-redirect" title="Hanged">hanged</a> by the neck from a railcar-mounted industrial crane.<sup id="cite_ref-335" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-335">&#91;335&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-336" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-336">&#91;336&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Unnamed cow
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>January 1932
</td>
<td>In January 1932, the Townsville Daily Bulletin, an Australian newspaper, reported an incident where a dairy cow was partially blown up and killed on a farm at Kennedy Creek (near Cardwell, North Queensland). The cow had reputedly picked up a detonator in her mouth while grazing in a paddock. This was only triggered later, when the cow began to chew her cud, at a time when she was in the process of being milked. The cow had its head blown off by the resulting explosion, and the farmer milking the cow was knocked unconscious.<sup id="cite_ref-337" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-337">&#91;337&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Unnamed deer
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>August 1987
</td>
<td>Stefan Johansson hit a deer with his McLaren MP4/3 after it wandered onto the circuit during Friday practice. The terrified deer was crossing the track to seek refuge from the noise of the cars when it was struck by Johansson traveling at close to 140&#160;mph (225&#160;km/h), killing it instantly.<sup id="cite_ref-338" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-338">&#91;338&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Royal the dog
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>September 1993
</td>
<td>Philip Rinn's dog, Royal, tried to bite Rinn's wife and had chewed part of Rinn's car. Rinn tied a chain around its neck and dragged it around with his Chrysler, but the dog did not die. Rinn then ran over the dog a few times before it died.<sup id="cite_ref-339" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-339">&#91;339&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Unnamed bird
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>March 24, 2001
</td>
<td>During a <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> spring training game, pitcher <a href="/wiki/Randy_Johnson" title="Randy Johnson">Randy Johnson</a> threw a fastball just as a bird flew through the pitch's path. The bird was killed instantly.<sup id="cite_ref-340" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-340">&#91;340&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-341" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-341">&#91;341&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Unnamed feral pigeon
</th>
<td>
</td>
<td>29 May 2009
</td>
<td>During a <a href="/wiki/Twenty20" title="Twenty20">Twenty20</a> cricket match at <a href="/wiki/Headingley_Cricket_Ground" title="Headingley Cricket Ground">Headingley Cricket Ground</a>, Leeds, England between Yorkshire and Lancashire, <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Rudolph" title="Jacques Rudolph">Jacques Rudolph</a> of Yorkshire fielded a ball close to the midwicket boundary and threw it to the wicket keeper. The return throw struck and killed a pigeon in flight across the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-342" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-342">&#91;342&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-343" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-343">&#91;343&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<li id="cite_note-Johnston1806b-66"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Johnston1806b_66-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite id="CITEREFWanleyJohnston1806" class="citation book">Wanley, Nathaniel; Johnston, William (1806). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/wondersoflittlew00wanluoft#page/n111">"Chapter XXVIII: Of the different and unusual Ways by which some Men have come to their Deaths §&#8239;29"</a>. <i>Book I: Which treats of the Perfections, Powers, Capacities, Defects, Imperfections, and Deformities of the Body of Man</i>. <i>The Wonders of the Little World; Or, A General History of Man: Displaying the Various Faculties, Capacities, Powers and Defects of the Human Body and Mind, in Many Thousand Most Interesting Relations of Persons Remarkable for Bodily Perfections or Defects; Collected from the Writings of the Most Approved Historians, Philosophers, and Physicians, of All Ages and Countries</i>. <b>1</b> (A new ed.). London. p.&#160;114. <a href="/wiki/ASIN_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="ASIN (identifier)">ASIN</a>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.amazon.com/dp/B001F3H1XA">B001F3H1XA</a>. <a href="/wiki/LCCN_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="LCCN (identifier)">LCCN</a>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//lccn.loc.gov/07003035">07003035</a>. <a href="/wiki/OCLC_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="OCLC (identifier)">OCLC</a>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.worldcat.org/oclc/847968918">847968918</a>. <a href="/wiki/OL_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="OL (identifier)">OL</a>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//openlibrary.org/books/OL7188480M">7188480M</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160829203137/https://archive.org/stream/wondersoflittlew00wanluoft#page/n111">Archived</a> from the original on 29 August 2016. <q>Charles II. King of Navarre, by a vicious life in his youth, fell into a paralytic distemper in his old age, that took away the use of his limbs. His physicians directed him to be sewed up in a sheet that had for a considerable time been steeped in strong distilled spirits, to recover the natural heat of his benumbed joints. The surgeon having sewed him up very close, and wanting a knife to cut off the thread, made use of a candle that was at hand to burn it off; but the flame from the thread reaching the sheet, the spirits wherewith it was wet immediately taking fire, burnt so vehemently, that no endeavours could extinguish the flame. Thus the miserable King lost his life in using the means to recover his health.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.atitle=Chapter+XXVIII%3A+Of+the+different+and+unusual+Ways+by+which+some+Men+have+come+to+their+Deaths+%C2%A7%26%238239%3B29&amp;rft.btitle=Book+I%3A+Which+treats+of+the+Perfections%2C+Powers%2C+Capacities%2C+Defects%2C+Imperfections%2C+and+Deformities+of+the+Body+of+Man&amp;rft.place=London&amp;rft.pages=114&amp;rft.edition=A+new&amp;rft.date=1806&amp;rft_id=info%3Aoclcnum%2F847968918&amp;rft_id=info%3Alccn%2F07003035&amp;rft.aulast=Wanley&amp;rft.aufirst=Nathaniel&amp;rft.au=Johnston%2C+William&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fstream%2Fwondersoflittlew00wanluoft%23page%2Fn111&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+unusual+deaths" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r951705291"/></span>

Retrieved <span class="nowrap">30 November</span> 2010</span>. <q>At the time of Tycho's death, in 1601, the blame fell on his failure to relieve himself while drinking profusely at the banquet, supposedly injuring his bladder and making him unable to urinate.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=The+New+York+Times&amp;rft.atitle=Murder%21+Intrigue%21+Astronomers%3F&amp;rft.date=2010-11-29&amp;rft.au=John+Tierney&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.nytimes.com%2F2010%2F11%2F30%2Fscience%2F30tierney.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+unusual+deaths" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r951705291"/></span>

<li id="cite_note-Murray2003-132"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Murray2003_132-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite id="CITEREFMurray2003" class="citation web">Murray, John (20 July 2003). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20030810022829/http://enjoyment.independent.co.uk/books/reviews/story.jsp?story=426412">"<i>Do Not Adjust Your Set</i>&#8239; By Kate Dunn: Live television drama may have gone, but, says Matthew Sweet, this entertaining history ensures it won't be forgotten"</a>. <i>The Independent</i>. London. <a href="/wiki/ISSN_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="ISSN (identifier)">ISSN</a>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.worldcat.org/issn/0951-9467">0951-9467</a>. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://enjoyment.independent.co.uk/books/reviews/story.jsp?story=426412">the original</a> on 10 August 2003. <q>An incident on the set of a 1958 edition of Armchair Theatre illustrates the perverse extremes of professionalism that television actors were expected to exhibit. The ... cast included ... a young Welsh actor named Gareth Jones. 'During transmission', recalls &#91;Peter&#93; Bowles, 'a little group of us was talking on camera while awaiting the arrival of Gareth Jones's character [...] We could see him coming up towards us, and he was going to arrive on cue, but we saw him drop, we saw him fall. We had no idea what had happened, but he certainly wasn't coming our way. The actors, including me, started making up lines: "I'm sure if So‑and‑so were here he would say..."' Jones had suffered a fatal heart attack—but rather than informing the actors of their colleague's death and ceasing transmission of the play, the producers decided to let them stumble on to the end.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=The+Independent&amp;rft.atitle=Do+Not+Adjust+Your+Set%26%238239%3B+By+Kate+Dunn%3A+Live+television+drama+may+have+gone%2C+but%2C+says+Matthew+Sweet%2C+this+entertaining+history+ensures+it+won%27t+be+forgotten&amp;rft.date=2003-07-20&amp;rft.issn=0951-9467&amp;rft.aulast=Murray&amp;rft.aufirst=John&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fenjoyment.independent.co.uk%2Fbooks%2Freviews%2Fstory.jsp%3Fstory%3D426412&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+unusual+deaths" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r951705291"/></span>
